    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex
>           raise last_ex.with_traceback(None)

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,

        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex
>           raise last_ex.with_traceback(None)

        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:

                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex

                break

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break

            assert last_ex

    @classmethod
    def connect(
        cls,
        conninfo: str = "",
        *,
        autocommit: bool = False,
        prepare_threshold: int | None = 5,
        context: AdaptContext | None = None,
        row_factory: RowFactory[Row] | None = None,
        cursor_factory: type[Cursor[Row]] | None = None,
        **kwargs: ConnParam,
    ) -> Self:
        """
        Connect to a database server and return a new `Connection` instance.
        """
    
        params = cls._get_connection_params(conninfo, **kwargs)
        timeout = timeout_from_conninfo(params)
        rv = None
        attempts = conninfo_attempts(params)
        for attempt in attempts:
            try:
                conninfo = make_conninfo("", **attempt)
                gen = cls._connect_gen(conninfo, timeout=timeout)
                rv = waiting.wait_conn(gen, interval=_WAIT_INTERVAL)
            except e._NO_TRACEBACK as ex:
                if len(attempts) > 1:
                    logger.debug(
                        "connection attempt failed: host: %r port: %r, hostaddr %r: %s",
                        attempt.get("host"),
                        attempt.get("port"),
                        attempt.get("hostaddr"),
                        str(ex),
                    )
                last_ex = ex
            else:
                break
    
        if not rv:
            assert last_ex
